==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: Position literals first in all String comparison methods: non-overloaded 'boolean equals(Object o)' and 'equalsIgnoreCase' and 'compareTo' and 'compareToIgnoreCase' and 'contentEquals', if the second argument is null then NullPointerExceptions can be avoided, they will just return false.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// bad, literal comes last in .equals comparison
public class Foo {
    boolean bar(String x) {
        return x.equals("2");
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 1
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();
        if (methodName.equals("equals") || methodName.equals("equalsIgnoreCase") 
            || methodName.equals("compareTo") || methodName.equals("compareToIgnoreCase") 
            || methodName.equals("contentEquals")) {
            Node firstChild = node.jjtGetChild(0);
            if (!(firstChild instanceof ASTStringLiteral)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node) && isLiteralSecond(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(ASTMethodCall node) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();
        return methodName.equals("equals") || methodName.equals("equalsIgnoreCase") || methodName.equals("compareTo") || methodName.equals("compareToIgnoreCase") || methodName.equals("contentEquals");
    }

    private boolean isLiteralSecond(ASTMethodCall node) {
        if (node.jjtGetNumChildren() > 1) {
            return node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess && node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTStringLiteral;
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node)) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess && node.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(ASTMethodCall node) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();
        return methodName.equals("equals")
                || methodName.equals("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equals("compareTo")
                || methodName.equals("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equals("contentEquals");
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node.getMethodName())) {
            if (node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null && 
                node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class) != null) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(String methodName) {
        return "equals".equals(methodName) || "equalsIgnoreCase".equals(methodName)
                || "compareTo".equals(methodName) || "compareToIgnoreCase".equals(methodName)
                || "contentEquals".equals(methodName);
    }
}

==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: Position literals first in all String comparison methods: non-overloaded 'boolean equals(Object o)' and 'equalsIgnoreCase' and 'compareTo' and 'compareToIgnoreCase' and 'contentEquals', if the second argument is null then NullPointerExceptions can be avoided, they will just return false.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// ok, empty literal in .equals comparison
public class Foo {
    void bar(String str) {
        if ((str == null) || (str.equals(""))) {
            str = "snafu";
        }
        if (str == null || str.equals("")) {
            str = "snafu";
        }
        if ((str != null) && (str.equals(""))) {
            str = "snafu";
        }
        if (str != null && str.equals("")) {
            str = "snafu";
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 2
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 4

```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node)) {
            if (node.getChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess && node.getArgumentCount() > 0 
              && node.getArgument(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(ASTMethodCall methodCall) {
        String methodName = methodCall.getMethodName();
        return  methodName.equals("equals") || methodName.equals("equalsIgnoreCase") ||
                methodName.equals("compareTo") || methodName.equals("compareToIgnoreCase") ||
                methodName.equals("contentEquals");
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private static final String LITERALS_FIRST_IN_COMPARISONS_RULE = "Position literals first in String comparison methods";

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node.getMethodName())) {
            if (isSecondArgumentLiteral(node)) {
                addViolationWithMessage(data, node, LITERALS_FIRST_IN_COMPARISONS_RULE);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(String methodName) {
        return methodName.equals("equals") 
            || methodName.equals("equalsIgnoreCase") 
            || methodName.equals("compareTo") 
            || methodName.equals("compareToIgnoreCase") 
            || methodName.equals("contentEquals");
    }

    private boolean isSecondArgumentLiteral(ASTMethodCall node) {
        ASTArgumentList arguments = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArgumentList.class);
        if (arguments != null && arguments.jjtGetNumChildren() > 1) {
            return arguments.jjtGetChild(1).getClass().getSimpleName().equals("ASTStringLiteral");
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node)) {
            Node firstArgument = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArgumentList.class).getChild(0);
            if (firstArgument instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(ASTMethodCall node) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();
        return "equals".equals(methodName) || "equalsIgnoreCase".equals(methodName) ||
                "compareTo".equals(methodName) || "compareToIgnoreCase".equals(methodName) ||
                "contentEquals".equals(methodName);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private static final String EQUALS = "equals";
    private static final String EQUALS_IGNORE_CASE = "equalsIgnoreCase";
    private static final String COMPARE_TO = "compareTo";
    private static final String COMPARE_TO_IGNORE_CASE = "compareToIgnoreCase";
    private static final String CONTENT_EQUALS = "contentEquals";

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        // Check if the method is one of the comparison methods
        if (EQUALS.equals(methodName)
                || EQUALS_IGNORE_CASE.equals(methodName)
                || COMPARE_TO.equals(methodName)
                || COMPARE_TO_IGNORE_CASE.equals(methodName)
                || CONTENT_EQUALS.equals(methodName)) {

            // Ensure that the first argument is a literal
            Node firstArgument = node.getArgument(0);
            if (!(firstArgument instanceof ASTLiteral)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node) && !isLiteralFirstArgument(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(ASTMethodCall node) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();
        return methodName.equals("equals") || methodName.equals("equalsIgnoreCase") || methodName.equals("compareTo")
                || methodName.equals("compareToIgnoreCase") || methodName.equals("contentEquals");
    }

    private boolean isLiteralFirstArgument(ASTMethodCall node) {
        if (node.getArguments().size() != 1) {
            return false;
        }
        return node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral;
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTPrimaryExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTPrimaryExpression node, Object data) {
        Node firstChild = node.jjtGetChild(0);

        if (firstChild instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = (ASTMethodCall) firstChild;

            if (isViolation(methodCall.getMethodName())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isViolation(String methodName) {
        return "equalsIgnoreCase".equals(methodName) || "equals".equals(methodName) || "compareTo".equals(methodName) ||
                "compareToIgnoreCase".equals(methodName) || "contentEquals".equals(methodName);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node)) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            ASTStringLiteral stringLiteral = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class);

            if (variableAccess != null && stringLiteral != null) {
                int variableAccessIndex = node.jjtGetChildIndex(variableAccess);
                int stringLiteralIndex = node.jjtGetChildIndex(stringLiteral);

                if (variableAccessIndex < stringLiteralIndex) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(ASTMethodCall node) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();
        return methodName.equals("equals") ||
                methodName.equals("equalsIgnoreCase") ||
                methodName.equals("compareTo") ||
                methodName.equals("compareToIgnoreCase") ||
                methodName.equals("contentEquals");
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node)) {
            ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpression = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTPrimaryExpression.class);
            if (primaryExpression != null && primaryExpression.jjtGetNumChildren() > 0 
                && primaryExpression.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(ASTMethodCall methodCall) {
        String methodName = methodCall.getMethodName();
        return "equals".equals(methodName) ||
                "equalsIgnoreCase".equals(methodName) ||
                "compareTo".equals(methodName) ||
                "compareToIgnoreCase".equals(methodName) ||
                "contentEquals".equals(methodName);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }
    
    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class)) {
            ASTStringLiteral literal = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class);
            if (literal.jjtGetParent().jjtGetChildIndex() > node.jjtGetChildIndex()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node)) {
            if (node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0 && node.getArguments().get(0).getClass() != ASTStringLiteral.class) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(ASTMethodCall node) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();
        return "equals".equals(methodName) || "equalsIgnoreCase".equals(methodName)
                || "compareTo".equals(methodName) || "compareToIgnoreCase".equals(methodName)
                || "contentEquals".equals(methodName);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    
    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTMethodDeclaration.class, ASTReturnStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (node.getResultType().isBoolean()) {
            super.visit(node, data);
        }
        return data;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTReturnStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = (ASTMethodCall) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            String methodName = methodCall.getMethodName();
            if (methodName.equals("compareTo") || methodName.equals("compareToIgnoreCase") ||
                    methodName.equals("equals") || methodName.equals("equalsIgnoreCase") || methodName.equals("contentEquals")) {
                if (methodCall.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return data;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node)) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).jjtGetChildIndex() < node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).jjtGetChildIndex()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(ASTMethodCall node) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();
        return methodName.equals("equals")
                || methodName.equals("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equals("compareTo")
                || methodName.equals("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equals("contentEquals");
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node)) {
            if (isLiteralSecondArgument(node)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(ASTMethodCall node) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        return methodName.equals("equals") || methodName.equals("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equals("compareTo") || methodName.equals("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equals("contentEquals");
    }

    private boolean isLiteralSecondArgument(ASTMethodCall node) {
        if (node.getArgumentCount() > 1) {
            return node.getArgument(1) instanceof ASTStringLiteral;
        }

        return false;
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        if (isStringComparisonMethod(node) && isLiteralLastInComparison(node)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isStringComparisonMethod(ASTMethodCall node) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();
        return "equals".equals(methodName) || "equalsIgnoreCase".equals(methodName) 
            || "compareTo".equals(methodName) || "compareToIgnoreCase".equals(methodName)
            || "contentEquals".equals(methodName);
    }

    private boolean isLiteralLastInComparison(ASTMethodCall node) {
        return node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess && node.jjtGetChild(1).jjtGetChild(0).isStringLiteral();
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super();
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null
                    && node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTArgumentList.class).getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {

            ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpression = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTPrimaryExpression.class);
            if (primaryExpression != null) {
                ASTPrimaryPrefix primaryPrefix = primaryExpression.getFirstChildOfType(ASTPrimaryPrefix.class);
                if (primaryPrefix != null) {
                    ASTStringLiteral literal = primaryPrefix.getFirstChildOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class);
                    if (literal == null) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {

            if(node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if(node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).getBeginLine() < node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTLiteral.class).getBeginLine()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (isVariableFirstArgument(node)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isVariableFirstArgument(ASTMethodCall node) {
        return node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null &&
               node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).getParent().equals(node.getFirstChild());
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                ASTArgumentList argumentList = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArgumentList.class);
                if (argumentList != null && argumentList.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTLiteral) {
                    // if the argument is a literal, then no violation
                    return super.visit(node, data);
                }
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            ASTArgumentList args = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArgumentList.class);
            if (args != null && args.size() > 0) {
                if (args.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTLiteral.class) == null) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                } else if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).getBeginLine() 
                           < node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTLiteral.class).getBeginLine()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getTarget() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && !(node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTLiteral)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;
```

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTLiteral.class) != null) {
                if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTLiteral.class).getParent().getIndexInParent() == 0) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {

            ASTArgumentList argList = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArgumentList.class);

            if (argList != null && argList.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) != null) {
                ASTArgumentList argList = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArgumentList.class);
                if (argList.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTLiteral) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {

            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null &&
                    node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTLiteral.class) != null) {
                if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).getBeginLine() <
                        node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTLiteral.class).getBeginLine()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {

            ASTArgumentList arguments = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArgumentList.class);
            if (arguments != null && arguments.size() > 0) {
                if (!(arguments.get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;

                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {

            ASTArgumentList argumentList = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArgumentList.class);
            if (argumentList != null && argumentList.jjtGetNumChildren() > 0) {
                if (argumentList.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                } else if (argumentList.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
                    ASTMethodCall childMethodCall = (ASTMethodCall) argumentList.jjtGetChild(0);
                    if (childMethodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class) != null) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTArgumentList) {
                ASTArgumentList arguments = (ASTArgumentList) node.jjtGetChild(0);
                if (!arguments.jjtGetChild(0).getImage().startsWith("\"")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            } else if (!(node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null || node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0 && !(node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {

            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0 && node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                    AbstractJavaNode target = (AbstractJavaNode) node.getTarget();

                    if (!(target instanceof ASTMethodCall) && !(target instanceof ASTStringLiteral)) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

===============================新加一个测试用例生成的checker repair_test_error_query_when_testing==========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Position literals first in all String comparison methods: non-overloaded 'boolean equals(Object o)' and 'equalsIgnoreCase' and 'compareTo' and 'compareToIgnoreCase' and 'contentEquals', if the second argument is null then NullPointerExceptions can be avoided, they will just return false.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0 && node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        if(node.getTarget().getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    // Check if variable is the caller and literal is the argument
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } 
                    // Check if variable is the argument and literal is the caller
                    else if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class) != null) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {

            if (node.getTarget() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            } else if (node.getTarget() instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                // no violation
            } else {
                // in all other cases, add a violation
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class).equals(node.getArguments().get(0))) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

Rule description: Position literals first in all String comparison methods: non-overloaded 'boolean equals(Object o)' and 'equalsIgnoreCase' and 'compareTo' and 'compareToIgnoreCase' and 'contentEquals', if the second argument is null then NullPointerExceptions can be avoided, they will just return false.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {

            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            } 
            else if (node.getTarget() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                if (node.getArguments().isEmpty() || !(node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super();
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || 
            methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase") || 
            methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") ||
            methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase") || 
            methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            
            if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess &&
                    node.getTarget() instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryExpression.class) != null) {
                Node primaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryExpression.class);
                if (primaryExpression.jjtGetNumChildren() > 1 && primaryExpression.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTPrimaryPrefix) {
                    Node primaryPrefix = primaryExpression.jjtGetChild(0);
                    if (primaryPrefix.jjtGetNumChildren() > 0 && primaryPrefix.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTName) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            } else if (node.getTarget() != null && !(node.getTarget() instanceof ASTStringLiteral)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
```

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
```
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
```

                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            // Add a check for final modifier

                            }

                }
            }

```
    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
```

                            ASTFieldDeclaration fieldDeclaration =
                                    varAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTFieldDeclaration.class);
                            if (fieldDeclaration != null && !fieldDeclaration.isFinal()) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

```
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            // Check if the variable is a non-static field
                            ASTFieldDeclaration fieldDeclaration = varAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTFieldDeclaration.class);
                            if (fieldDeclaration == null || fieldDeclaration.isStatic()) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
