package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            Node parent = varAccess.getParent();
                            while (parent != null && !(parent instanceof ASTFieldDeclaration)) {
                                parent = parent.getParent();
                            }
                            if (parent != null) {
                                ASTFieldDeclaration field = (ASTFieldDeclaration) parent;
                                boolean isFinal = field.isFinal();
                                boolean isStatic = field.isStatic();
                                if (!isFinal || isStatic) {
                                    addViolation(data, node);
                                }
                            } else {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            ASTFieldDeclaration fieldDeclaration = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTFieldDeclaration.class);
                            if (fieldDeclaration != null) {
                                if (fieldDeclaration.getModifiers().isStatic()) {
                                    addViolation(data, node);
                                }
                            } else {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;

import java.util.Set;
import java.util.HashSet;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Set<String> nonStaticFields = new HashSet<>();

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFieldDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isStatic()) {
            nonStaticFields.add(node.getVariableName());
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();
        
        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty() &&
                            !nonStaticFields.contains(varAccess.getVariableName())) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;

        super(ASTMethodCall.class);

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {

                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            ASTClassOrInterfaceType variableType = (ASTClassOrInterfaceType) varAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTClassOrInterfaceType.class);
                            if (variableType != null && variableType.getType().getName().equals("String")) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        Scope scope = varAccess.getScope();
                        NameOccurrence nameOccurrence = scope.getDeclarations().get(varAccess.getImage());
                        if (nameOccurrence != null) {
                            if (nameOccurrence.isFinal()) {
                                return super.visit(node, data);
                            }
                        }
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    } else if (!(node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral)) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {

            if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                    ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                    if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                        for (NameOccurrence no : varAccess.getUsages()) {
                            VariableNameDeclaration vnd = no.getVariableNameDeclaration();
                            if (vnd.getAccessNodeParent().isFinal() && vnd.getAccessNodeParent().isStatic() && vnd.getTypeImage().equals("String")) {
                                return super.visit(node, data);
                            }
                        }
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;

import java.util.List;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            List<ASTFieldDeclaration> fields = varAccess.getFirstParentOfType(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class).findDescendantsOfType(ASTFieldDeclaration.class);
                            boolean isConstant = false;

                            for (ASTFieldDeclaration field : fields) {
                                if (field.getVariableName().equals(varAccess.getVariableName()) && field.isFinal() && field.isStatic()) {
                                    isConstant = true;
                                    break;
                                }
                            }

                            if (!isConstant) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.Set;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    private Set<String> constantNames = new HashSet<>();

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTFieldDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (node.isFinal() && node.isStatic()) {
            ASTVariableDeclarator declarator = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableDeclarator.class);
            if (declarator != null) {
                constantNames.add(declarator.getName());
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (!constantNames.contains(varAccess.getVariableName())) {
                            if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;



import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            if (!varAccess.isFinal()) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty() && !isConstant(varAccess)) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isConstant(ASTVariableAccess varAccess) {
        return varAccess.getNameDeclaration().isFinal() && varAccess.getNameDeclaration().isStatic();
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (!varAccess.getNameDeclaration().isFinal() && varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty() && !varAccess.isConstant()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpression = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTPrimaryExpression.class);
                            if (primaryExpression != null) {
                                ASTPrimaryPrefix primaryPrefix = primaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryPrefix.class);
                                if (primaryPrefix != null && primaryPrefix.usesThisModifier()) {
                                    addViolation(data, node);
                                }
                            } else {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import java.util.List;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    Node firstArgument = node.getArguments().get(0);
                    if (firstArgument instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) firstArgument;
                        if (!isConstant(varAccess)) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    } else if (!(firstArgument instanceof AbstractJavaNode && ((AbstractJavaNode) firstArgument).isConstant())) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isConstant(ASTVariableAccess varAccess) {
        List<ASTFieldDeclaration> fieldDeclarations = varAccess.getParent().findDescendantsOfType(ASTFieldDeclaration.class);
        for (ASTFieldDeclaration fieldDeclaration : fieldDeclarations) {
            if (fieldDeclaration.getVariableName().equals(varAccess.getVariableName())) {
                return fieldDeclaration.isFinal() && fieldDeclaration.isStatic();
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            if(node.getTarget() instanceof ASTFieldAccess && varAccess.isConstant()) {
                                // If method is called on a constant and the argument is also a constant, no NullPointerException can occur
                                // So skip the violation
                                return data;
                            }
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodCall.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodCall node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
                if (node.getArguments().size() > 0) {
                    if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                        ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    } else if (node.getArguments().get(0) instanceof ASTFieldAccess) {
                        ASTFieldAccess fieldAccess = (ASTFieldAccess) node.getArguments().get(0);
                        if (fieldAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.bestpractices;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public LiteralsFirstInComparisonsRule() {
        super(ASTMethodDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTMethodDeclaration node, Object data) {
        String methodName = node.getMethodName();

        if (methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equals") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("equalsIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareTo") || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("compareToIgnoreCase")
                || methodName.equalsIgnoreCase("contentEquals")) {
            if (node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArgumentList.class) != null) {
                ASTArgumentList argsList = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArgumentList.class);
                if (argsList.size() > 0 && (argsList.get(0) instanceof ASTStringLiteral
                        || argsList.get(0) instanceof ASTFieldAccess)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                } else if (argsList.size() > 0 && argsList.get(0) instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                    ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) argsList.get(0);
                    if (varAccess.findDescendantsOfType(ASTStringLiteral.class).isEmpty()) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
